 var step  = parseInt(dataEl.getAttribute('data-step')||'4');
 var grid  = container.querySelector('.nabd-grid');
 var next  = items.slice(shown, shown+step);
 next.forEach(function(it){
 var art = document.createElement('article');
 art.className='nabd-row';
 var img = it.image ? '<img class="nabd-thumb" loading="lazy" src="'+it.image+'" alt="">' : '';
 var meta = it.date_human ? '<div class="nabd-meta"><span>'+it.date_human+'</span></div>' : '';
 art.innerHTML = img + '<div class="nabd-text"><h3 class="nabd-title"><a href="'+it.link+'" target="_blank" rel="noopener">'+it.title+'</a></h3>'+meta+'</div>';
 grid.appendChild(art);
 });
 shown += next.length;
 dataEl.setAttribute('data-shown', shown);
 var btn = container.querySelector('.nabd-btn');
 if(shown >= items.length && btn){ btn.setAttribute('disabled','disabled'); }
 }
 document.addEventListener('click', function(e){
 var btn = e.target.closest('.nabd-btn');
 if(!btn) return;
 var wrap = btn.closest('.nabd-wrap');
 if(!wrap) return;
 e.preventDefault();
 render(wrap);
 });
 // auto render first batch for all instances
 document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){
 document.querySelectorAll('.nabd-wrap').forEach(render);
 });
 })();
